<div id="review_973985425" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/973985425" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/973985425?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer973985425" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3409026810130133973"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/edinburgh-at-dusk.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591986._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo edinburgh-at-dusk.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i> “So are you a hero, Cole Walker?”<br/>“What is a hero, really?”<br/>“I suppose it’s someone that saves people.”<br/>“Yeah, I suppose it is.”<br/>“So do you save people?”<br/>“I’m only fifteen. Give me a chance.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>And yet another fantastic romance from Samantha Young!!! For those of you who are following the <i>On Dublin Street</i> series, this is <b>Cole Walker’s</b> story. Jo’s now hot and sexy little brother. He has definitely grow out of that broody teenage kid stage, and is now working as a highly sou</span>
  <span id="freeText3409026810130133973" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/edinburgh-at-dusk.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591986._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo edinburgh-at-dusk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i> “So are you a hero, Cole Walker?”<br>“What is a hero, really?”<br>“I suppose it’s someone that saves people.”<br>“Yeah, I suppose it is.”<br>“So do you save people?”<br>“I’m only fifteen. Give me a chance.”</i>
</b><br><br>And yet another fantastic romance from Samantha Young!!! For those of you who are following the <i>On Dublin Street</i> series, this is <b>Cole Walker’s</b> story. Jo’s now hot and sexy little brother. He has definitely grow out of that broody teenage kid stage, and is now working as a highly sought-out tattoo artist in Edinburgh’s famous <b>Inkarnate</b>. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/9EC2F04E-BED6-4D4E-A783-B8AA9A01F33F.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591987._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9EC2F04E-BED6-4D4E-A783-B8AA9A01F33F.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>And growing up under the influence of Cameron, Braden, Nate and Marcus, he has grown into quite a stunning young man. Although even with his cut body, his tattoos and his killer bad boy look, he has kept his heart pure. He is the real deal. He could have any woman he wanted, but he’s still looking for <i>the one</i> that would capture his heart. (or had he already met her nine year earlier?)<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/cintia_dicker_by_levan27-d6b6nqg.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591988._SX540_.png" alt=" photo cintia_dicker_by_levan27-d6b6nqg.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Shannon MacLeod</b> met him when she was only 15. It was on the porch of her Grandmother’s house on Scotland Street. She only spoke to him for a few minutes, but it was just long enough to feel it… <i>the pull</i>. And then, she would turn back to see him as she walked away and he would be gone. It would be her first bad decision in the line of the many.<br><br><b>
  <i> “As the old car took me away from Scotland Street amid his incessant chatter, I felt like fate had just handed me two cups and I’d stupidly drunk from the wrong one.” </i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/da185b1d6263ba92526c35c085aabbf5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591989._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo da185b1d6263ba92526c35c085aabbf5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Shannon had a type. She always went for the bad boys. And she was always getting burned. Until the last one almost destroyed her, and the one she cared about most. So no more. Ever.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Those eyes crinkled attractively at the corners as their gorgeous owner threw me a friendly, boyish smile that penetrated my anti-bad-boy force field.” </i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/jedburgh.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591990._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo jedburgh.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After a falling out with her family, she relocated to Edinburgh, and was looking for work. She had given up her chance to go to art school, so her choices for were limited. The one ad she found that suited her just happened to be another tattoo parlor job. Not a good idea, since she was steering clear of men. And especially that type. But she had to find work, and soon.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/inkarnate_in_light_by_inkarnate.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591991._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo inkarnate_in_light_by_inkarnate.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Inkarnate had a fantastic reputation. She would be lucky to land a job like that, at least until something else came along. So she took it. But little did she know that the lead artist and manager was going to be a ghost from her past. Those same light green eyes that she turned her back on nine years ago. The ones she never forgot.<br><br><b>
  <i>I got a brief glimpse of strong, broad shoulders and long legs before he turned and my eyes collided with his bright green ones. Holy… My stomach plummeted. Dread filled me. Please, no, no, no. Be a customer. Please be a customer…</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/tumblr_m70b20xpvz1rtcoyto1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591992._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_m70b20xpvz1rtcoyto1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And apparently neither did he. Fate has a wicked sense of humor. Because she does not need this in her life right now. But really she does, she just doesn’t know it. <br><br>When Cole and Shannon meet again the sparks fly just as before, and where he can’t believe his good luck, she can’t believe her bad. <br><br><b>
  <i>“His lips were at my ear again. “Do you want me, Shannon?”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/hqdefault.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591993.jpg" alt=" photo hqdefault.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “Are you going to kill me with your magical hair?” I rubbed a strand of hair between my finger and thumb. “It is thick. It would make a good rope.” <br>“Dark. I like it, wee fairy.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/il_570xN55718509.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591994._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo il_570xN55718509.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really loved this story. Cole was such a great character. Growing up as he did, he really turned out to be a great guy. Not surprising with the mentors that adopted him along the way. But he still has scars from a mother who abused him growing up. And it is these scars that he finds a way to make such a difference in Shannon’s life.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/03310756-384B-4766-9686-47246C8AAB48_1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591995._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 03310756-384B-4766-9686-47246C8AAB48_1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “Shannon, there is nothing casual about how I feel about you. There hasn’t been since the day I stepped out of Ellie and Adam’s house and found you on the stoop. I get you don’t trust me and I get why, but I want you to give me the chance to change that. I think there’s something here that’s worth the effort.”</i>
</b><br><br>After suffering the trauma’s of her past, Shannon is justifiably wary of starting a relationship with anyone, and especially one who looks like Cole. She refuses to make yet another bad decision. But after getting to know him again, and learning to trust him, she can’t hold herself back any longer. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/07342370-6739-0131-706b-7ed2bd0de129.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591996.jpg" alt=" photo 07342370-6739-0131-706b-7ed2bd0de129.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “First, looking at your gorgeous artwork gave me a serious hard-on. I do love a talented woman. Second, I’m going to fuck every bad memory of those unworthy hits out of you, even if it takes me a lifetime. Starting tonight.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/2db4c56282fdec8c0623abce147d17e2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400105930i/9635752.jpg" alt=" photo 2db4c56282fdec8c0623abce147d17e2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>He turns out to be everything she’s looked for and everything she needs. Now, she just has to get over her guilt of finding happiness and to convince her family to trust her choices. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/381DD288-7F39-42E3-A593-7BBB24D35C3C.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413997314i/11591997._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 381DD288-7F39-42E3-A593-7BBB24D35C3C.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was a lovely story. The only issue I had was the misunderstanding between Cole and Shannon at the end. It was thrown way out of proportion by Cole, and not handled very well by he, Rae or Shannon. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And then, for her to go and propose right away, it just was a bit rushed for me. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Other than that, I loved it all. One of my favorite characters was Rae, Shannon’s new flat mate, and co-worker. But I also loved Simon and Tony. Pleased as pie!<br><br><b>
  <i> “I love you, Shannon. I want to protect you and keep you safe. I want to be your family and to give you mine so that you never have to feel sad about anyone who is too stupid to realize they’ve let go of something so special, their lives will always be a little darker for it.”</i>
</b><br><br>Can’t wait for her brother LOGAN’s STORY!!! BRING IT ON!!<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/559BC2FE-01B7-4EC5-AD36-8FD73E5F6C45.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413314721i/11495074._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 559BC2FE-01B7-4EC5-AD36-8FD73E5F6C45.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3409026810130133973" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2210020830" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2210020830" />
    <a title="Lover of Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance"><img alt="Lover of Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458253423p2/3709091.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2210020830?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lover of Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lover of Romance" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance">Lover of Romance</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22597117-echoes-of-scotland-street">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2210020830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7078292079302381222">This review was originally posted on<a href='http://addictedtoromance.org/2017/12/10/book-review-echoes-at-scotland-street-by-samantha-young/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'> Addicted To Romance</a><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512858742i/24639323._SX540_.png' alt='' width='600' height='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Another wonderful addition that Samantha Young brings to the Dublin Street series. We see so much growth in this group of family and friends that come together during the good and the hard times.<br/><br/><strong>Echoes At Scotland Street </strong>is a story that will lift your spirits but also push your emotional limits at times. Our delicious key players for this story are:<br/> <br/> 	 Cole Walker, our sexy bad boy hero, tattooed and charming and women chase him but at the </span>
  <span id="freeText7078292079302381222" style="display:none">This review was originally posted on<a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/2017/12/10/book-review-echoes-at-scotland-street-by-samantha-young/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> Addicted To Romance</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512858742i/24639323._SX540_.png" alt="" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Another wonderful addition that Samantha Young brings to the Dublin Street series. We see so much growth in this group of family and friends that come together during the good and the hard times.<br><br><strong>Echoes At Scotland Street </strong>is a story that will lift your spirits but also push your emotional limits at times. Our delicious key players for this story are:<br> <br> 	 Cole Walker, our sexy bad boy hero, tattooed and charming and women chase him but at the heart is a good guy with a heart of gold. <br> 	 Shannon MacLeod, our lovely heroine, spirited and been burned by bad boys and considers herself to have the worst luck in men. <br> <br>This story was pretty interesting to read and I have been admiring Cole for most of the series especially in seeing what a good brother he was to Jo--a heroine in book 2. We see in his true element, a talented artist working in a high end tattoo parlor. Now I haven't had the chance to read too many books that take place in a tattoo parlor and I found that Young did a wonderful job in writing up the set up of this story. Our heroine, is looking for a job and finds a secretarial job and runs into Cole, a boy she once knew when she was a teenager and felt a connection. But Shannon tends to think she has the worst luck in men, they tend to all be very toxic and betray her in one form or another and is estranged from her family. At first she makes a certain assumption about Cole, that he is like all the other men she has been with previously. Which causes some intense tension and our heroine has to prove to Cole how sorry she really is. Because Shannon soon realizes that Cole isn't the bad boy that he appears to be and appearances can be deceiving. But this isn't the first time that Shannon makes a mistake with Cole. And she will be faced with a difficult decision either her family or the man she loves?<br><blockquote>You’re worth every bad thing that’s ever happened to me, because going through them led me to you.</blockquote><br>What I found simply wonderful about this book that made the biggest impression on me was our hero. He was definitely dreamy and even though he is a bit of a playboy at times, he also is a good one, a true keeper. He also isn't as cocky as you would expect. In fact, our of all the heroes, this author has written, Cole is probably my favorite to read so far. There is something so compelling about his character, and how true he is to himself.  I truly adored the changes we see in our heroine. She has been burned so much in her life, and my heart really broke for her situation. So I tried not to judge her too harshly. What I respected about the way her character was written is how realistic she is. She really grows and learns to fight for herself and what she really wants in life and I just admired that. And she learns some tough lessons but I did like that she comes through for the reader and you learn to become endeared by her character.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512923327i/24646352.png" alt="" width="500" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512619583i/24620398._SX540_.png" alt="" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[foogallery id="21818"]<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512858742i/24639321._SX540_.png" alt="" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499527757i/23242699.jpg" alt=" photo Addicted To Romance Reviews 2_zpsplp8m0tb.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7078292079302381222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1728578028" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1728578028" />
    <a title="ambsreads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads"><img alt="ambsreads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508924675p2/30813900.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1728578028?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ambsreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ambsreads" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads">ambsreads</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer16919718627225453462">I'm going to avoid writing a full review for this book as well, mainly because I'm lazy. It was fluffy. It was sweet. It was adorable and full of angst. I loved the fact we got to see Cole grown up, he's been one of favourite characters since he was introduced. The book was an easy read with a similar story line to the rest of the books in the series, which ultimately made it enjoyable for me.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15383191094498476400">I loved Echoes of Scotland Street Cole and Shannon's story, they have their problems to work through before they have their HEA.<br/><br/>Shannon has come to Edinborough for a fresh start escaping her past and all her bad desicions. Shannon has her issues with trusting men especially if they have tattoos and the only place she has an interview is a tattoo studio INKarnate enter Cole and the story begins.<br/><br/>Cole Walker has grown up since we first met him in Down London Road. I guess spending 10 years around C</span>
  <span id="freeText15383191094498476400" style="display:none">I loved Echoes of Scotland Street Cole and Shannon's story, they have their problems to work through before they have their HEA.<br /><br />Shannon has come to Edinborough for a fresh start escaping her past and all her bad desicions. Shannon has her issues with trusting men especially if they have tattoos and the only place she has an interview is a tattoo studio INKarnate enter Cole and the story begins.<br /><br />Cole Walker has grown up since we first met him in Down London Road. I guess spending 10 years around Cam, Nate and Braden has rubbed off on Cole turning him into a strong, caring, loyal friend and sometimes he can be a bossy 25 year old man. Cole is looking for "the one" he does not do casual sex. <br /><br />Shannon and Cole's working relationship gets off on the wrong footing when Shannon say's hurtful things to Cole only to protect herself and Cole does not have the time of day for Shannon after that. Enter Hannah Cole's BF to give Shannon the true facts about Cole, soon Shannon discovers the real Cole under the tattoos not the bad boy she thought he was and this is where their relationship begins with all the hot sex.<br /><br />Love the gang at INKarnate they are all funny, great catching up with the rest of the clan from the other books. I did not like Shannon's family they were cold towards her with the exception of Logan Shannon's big brother which we will get to know better in his next book.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23384676-a-ryan?shelf=alpha-male-becomes-a-girl">alpha-male-becomes-a-girl</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1673532586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10495228915488162966">DNF @ 52%<br/><br/>This is Cole's story and the fifth installment of Samantha Young's <i> On Dublin Street </i> series. I have loved Cole since he was introduced in the second book and I was REALLY looking forward to his story.<br/><br/>But unfortunately, I'm just not connecting with these characters. Cole seems different somehow, too nice maybe? Or maybe a little too desperate for a serious relationship? I get the sense that he would fall just as completely for another woman, if Shannon hadn't come along. <br/><br/>Shannon seemed </span>
  <span id="freeText10495228915488162966" style="display:none">DNF @ 52%<br /><br />This is Cole's story and the fifth installment of Samantha Young's <i> On Dublin Street </i> series. I have loved Cole since he was introduced in the second book and I was REALLY looking forward to his story.<br /><br />But unfortunately, I'm just not connecting with these characters. Cole seems different somehow, too nice maybe? Or maybe a little too desperate for a serious relationship? I get the sense that he would fall just as completely for another woman, if Shannon hadn't come along. <br /><br />Shannon seemed rather dull. Apart from her hair, it was difficult to ascertain why she was so endearing. Her personality did not come through in any of her interactions with her friends or with Cole and Young focused mainly on her fear of trusting anyone.<br /><br />I'm a little disappointed, and while I usually hate not finishing a book... I just don't care about what happens next. <br /><br />I still recommend the series, particularly books 1, 2 and 3. (The third book being a stand out favourite of mine!) And I will certainly be reading more by this author.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10495228915488162966" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IEqo45aek3gohGxA23pqdniw+EMbq5m1jIhoSJo53ChhWhz5O664I0NJpHEpHAZhYeoUn+rqi5x3DTjxCYZn7w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('To0tIVBskf7B7tbXJvx2M7xmXwTrR0ifAp7FZyrHwB8PnZk7/Vy6paojHubUmhokpTyz2BoGWrb5G5XeuXh72A==')})
  }
//]]>
